Exxon,2017-11,UPDATE 2-Dutch court rejects government's Groningen gas production plan - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-11,{{20171115T142310.972+0000}}UPDATE 2-Dutch court rejects government's Groningen gas production plan(Adds reaction from Economic Affairs Ministry and gas extraction company NAM and more background)
Exxon,2017-11,"THE HAGUE, Nov 15 (Reuters) - The highest Dutch administrative court has rejected the government's plan to cap production at a major gas field that has caused damaging earthquakes, saying it might be possible to cut output further without endangering supplies."
Exxon,2017-11,"The decision adds another chapter to the long fight over gas production in the northern Dutch province of Groningen, where citizens accuse the government of endangering their lives while protecting gas revenues."
Exxon,2017-11,"The government had proposed capping production at the Groningen gas field at 21.6 billion cubic metres (bcm) per year over the next five years, after a 2015 report found production was risking lives. That would be down from 24 bcm in the production year just ended and 39.4 bcm in 2015-16. [nL8N19G55U]"
Exxon,2017-11,"But the Council of State said on Wednesday the government had failed to properly substantiate its decision, describing it as ""unacceptable"" to potentially keep production unchanged for five years when it might be possible to further reduce demand."
Exxon,2017-11,"The Council ordered the government to review its decision within the next 12 months, but production could be maintained at 21.6 bcm for the year through Oct. 1, 2018."
Exxon,2017-11,"The Economic Affairs Ministry called the verdict a ""tough decision"", but accepted it has to come up with a new plan in the coming year."
Exxon,2017-11,"The drafting of a new plan will be the responsibility of Economic Affairs minister Eric Wiebes, whose predecessor Henk Kamp left office when the new government was installed last month. Kamp lowered gas production in Groningen several times in response to earthquakes, but was still seen by residents as neglecting the risks of ongoing production."
Exxon,2017-11,"Wednesday's decision was met with jubilation from Groningen citizens, many of whom have seen their houses damaged by the thousands of small earthquakes triggered by the gas extraction."
Exxon,2017-11,"""We won on all fronts. All lousy excuses the government used to justify production have been tossed out the window,"" said Dirk Kleijer, a spokesman for the Groninger Bodembeweging campaign group."
Exxon,2017-11,"""The minister now needs to put the safety of residents first. He now needs to come up with a good plan: to lower production and to guarantee our safety""."
Exxon,2017-11,"NAM, the Royal Dutch Shell and ExxonMobil joint venture that operates the Groningen field, also found support in the court ruling, saying it affirmed its view that the safe level of production can be determined by using the right models."
Exxon,2017-11,"The NAM had contested the government's new production cap, saying it ignored earlier agreed safety norms."
Exxon,2017-11,"WASHINGTON, Nov 14 (Reuters) - The Republican and Democratic leaders of the U.S. Senate Foreign Relations Committee blasted the U.S. State Department on Tuesday for cuts in staff and what they described as a failure to have a plan for a proposed reorganization."
Exxon,2017-11,"""I don't think they are anywhere close to having a plan to present relative to the reforms that they want,"" said Senator Bob Corker, the Republican chairman of the committee."
Exxon,2017-11,"Rex Tillerson, Republican President Donald Trump's Secretary of State, has embraced the White House's proposal - rejected by key members of Congress - to cut the State Department budget by about 30 percent. He has imposed a hiring freeze while analyzing the agency's operations and deciding how to reorganize them."
Exxon,2017-11,"Tillerson, a former chief executive at Exxon Mobil Corp who took office on Feb. 1, has offered few specifics to ease concerns, including in Congress, that the plan risks weakening U.S. standing in the world."
Exxon,2017-11,"Senator Ben Cardin, the top Democrat on the Foreign Relations panel, called the staff reductions a risk to national security and a ""high-level decapitation of leadership."""
Exxon,2017-11,"""Folks, this situation is alarming. We put our country in danger,"" Cardin said during a committee business meeting."
Exxon,2017-11,"Corker said the panel had had ""a very unsatisfactory meeting last week with the State Department"" and that concern was bipartisan. ""We need to be much more focused on holding them accountable,"" Corker said."
Exxon,2017-11,"Trump has several times contradicted Tillerson on foreign policy issues. The president said earlier this month that his opinion was the only one that mattered in U.S. foreign policy. ""The one that matters is me,"" Trump said on Fox News. ""I'm the only one that matters because, when it comes to it, that's what the policy is going to be."" [nL2N1N9155]"

Exxon,2017-11,"Eni signs Oman oil and gas exploration deal, Qatari firm to take stake - Reuters News"
Exxon,2017-11,"{{20171114T113057.059+0000}}Eni signs Oman oil and gas exploration deal, Qatari firm to take stakeMILAN, Nov 14 (Reuters) - Italian energy firm Eni signed a deal on Tuesday to explore an area off the southern coast of Oman for oil and gas and inked an agreement for Qatar Petroleum (QP) to take a stake in the block."
Exxon,2017-11,"Under the Exploration and Production Sharing Agreement (EPSA), Eni will be operator of Block 52 with an initial 85 percent stake, with the rest held by a subsidiary of state-owned Oman Oil Company SAOC."
Exxon,2017-11,"But Eni said it had also signed an agreement to cede 30 percent of the block to Qatar Petroleum (QP), a move that will reduce the Italian firm's stake to 55 percent once completed."
Exxon,2017-11,"Selling down stakes in oil and gas fields it operates is part of Eni's so-called ""dual exploration"" strategy to raise cash to fund development and support dividends."
Exxon,2017-11,"""The signing of the Block 52 EPSA represents an important milestone in Eni's strategy to reinforce its presence in the Middle East region,"" Eni CEO Claudio Descalzi said."
Exxon,2017-11,Descalzi welcomed the deal with QP given its position as a top liquefied natural gas (LNG) operator.
Exxon,2017-11,"Eni, the biggest foreign oil producer in Africa, is seeking to develop its LNG business in an effort to find markets for its bumper gas discoveries in Mozambique and Egypt."
Exxon,2017-11,"Block 52, located in water depths ranging from 10 metres to over 2,000 metres, is largely underexplored, covering more than 90,000 square kilometres, QP said in a separate statement."
Exxon,2017-11,QP is seeking to expand overseas through joint ventures with international oil firms to maintain its dominance over rivals in the United States and Australia.
Exxon,2017-11,It will start drilling with ExxonMobil for oil and gas off the southern coast of Cyprus in 2018.
Exxon,2017-11,"UPDATE 1-Abu Dhabi to boost capacity of giant Upper Zakum, Bab oil fields - Reuters News"
Exxon,2017-11,"{{20171114T093450.935+0000}}UPDATE 1-Abu Dhabi to boost capacity of giant Upper Zakum, Bab oil fields(Adds expansion of capacity at second Abu Dhabi field)"
Exxon,2017-11,"DUBAI, Nov 14 (Reuters) - Abu Dhabi said on Tuesday that it would increase the capacity of its giant Upper Zakum offshore oil field, one of the world's largest, to 1 million barrels per day by 2024."
Exxon,2017-11,"An agreement for the project was signed between the government's Abu Dhabi National Oil Co (ADNOC), Exxon Mobil of the United States and Japan's Inpex Corp <1605.T>, ADNOC said."
Exxon,2017-11,"The Upper Zakum field is the second largest offshore oil field and fourth largest oil field in the world, the statement said. Previously, Abu Dhabi was pursuing a plan to boost its production capacity to 750,000 bpd by 2017-18."
Exxon,2017-11,"ADNOC also said it would upgrade operations at its onshore Bab field, increasing production capacity to 450,000 bpd by 2020 from 420,000 bpd."
Exxon,2017-11,"An engineering, procurement and construction contract for this project has been awarded to China Petroleum Engineering & Construction Corp, an affiliate of China National Petroleum."

Exxon,2017-11,UPDATE 1-Ghana opens talks with Exxon on deepwater drilling contract  - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-11,{{20171113T205644.817+0000}}UPDATE 1-Ghana opens talks with Exxon on deepwater drilling contract (Adds quotes and context)
Exxon,2017-11,"ACCRA, Nov 13 (Reuters) - Ghana has opened talks with Exxon Mobil Corp to allow the U.S. oil firm to undertake deepwater exploration off its coast, a deputy energy minister said on Monday."
Exxon,2017-11,"""The negotiations are ongoing according to our current laws ... so far so good,"" Mohamed Amin Adam told Reuters on the sidelines of an Africa oil conference in Accra."
Exxon,2017-11,"Adam said the government had opted for direct negotiation with Exxon Mobil without open competitive tendering due to the peculiar nature of the field, and because Ghana has yet to pass regulations to back open competitive tendering."
Exxon,2017-11,A new petroleum law requires that oil contracts should be awarded through open and competitive tender. It also allows direct negotiation when necessary and justifiable.
Exxon,2017-11,"Exxon Mobil signed a Memorandum of Understanding with Ghana in 2015 to assess its Deepwater Cape Three Point (DCTP) region, 150 km (100 miles) off the coast with water depth ranging between 2,000 and 4,000 metres (6,500 and 13,000 feet)."
Exxon,2017-11,The government said two firms had separately opted not to seek to explore the field because of its depth and high risk levels.
Exxon,2017-11,"Adam said the government considered the ExxonMobil bid important, given the firm's experience and capability in deepwater operations. ""Ultra-deepwater exploration is beyond the reach of current technology and we believe operators with strong research and development capability such as ExxonMobil are needed to unlock the potentials,"" Adam said."
Exxon,2017-11,The DCTP interest is the second attempt by Exxon Mobil to acquire oil assets in Ghana after the government blocked its 2009 bid to take over Kosmos' stake in the flagship Jubilee field.
Exxon,2017-11,"Ghana, which also produces cocoa and gold, expects to ramp up oil production to around 250,000 barrels per day by 2019 from four oil fields including Jubilee whose current combined average annual output is around 100,000 bpd."

Exxon,2017-11,"{{20171113T202141.530+0000}}Ghana opens talks with Exxon on deepwater drilling contract -deputy energy ministerACCRA, Nov 13 (Reuters) - Ghana has opened talks with Exxon Mobil Corp to allow the U.S. oil firm to undertake deepwater exploration off the West African nation's coast, a deputy energy minister said on Monday."
Exxon,2017-11,"""The negotiations are ongoing according to our current laws ... so far so good,"" Mohamed Amin Adam told Reuters on the sidelines of an Africa oil conference in Accra."

Exxon,2017-11,"* Urals crude differentials firmed against dated Brent in northwest Europe on Monday on demand for December volumes, though there were no loading dates for next month so far."
Exxon,2017-11,"* In the Platts window BP bid for 100,000 tonnes loading from Baltic ports on Dec. 3-7 at dated Brent minus $0.90 a barrel, which was around 15 cents firmer than the recent estimates, but failed to find a seller."
Exxon,2017-11,"* Traders said it was not easy to find a seller for December-loading cargo before the release of loading dates, which is expected over the course of the week."
Exxon,2017-11,* Urals December exports are expected to be even lower than in November due to higher runs on Russian refineries.
Exxon,2017-11,"* In the Mediterranean Litasco offered 140,000 tonnes of Urals loading from Novorossiisk on Nov. 23-27 at dated Brent minus $0.40 a barrel, but failed to find a buyer and withdrew the offer."
Exxon,2017-11,"* Traders said demand for 140,000-tonne cargoes in the Mediterranean was rather poor due to limited arbitrage possibilities to Asia."
Exxon,2017-11,* Premiums for CPC Blend against dated Brent remained stable despite ample supply expected for December.
Exxon,2017-11,"* In the Platts window OMV bid for 85,000 tonnes of CPC Blend loading on Nov. 29 - Dec. 2 at a premium of $0.25 a barrel, while Trafigura offered a cargo of the same size loading on Dec. 4-8 at dated Brent plus $0.40 a barrel, traders said."
Exxon,2017-11,"* Bids and offers were in line with the latest grade's estimates, but no deal was done."

Exxon,2017-11,UPDATE 1-Kashagan development delayed again over new output glitches - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-11,{{20171113T164506.161+0000}}UPDATE 1-Kashagan development delayed again over new output glitches(Adds more details)
Exxon,2017-11,"MOSCOW, Nov 13 (Reuters) - Kazakhstan's giant Kashagan oilfield will reach its planned capacity of 370,000 barrels per day later than anticipated, its developer, the North Caspian Operating Company (NCOC), said on Monday."
Exxon,2017-11,"""I expect that we will need year 2018 to fully accomplish this (370,000 bpd) capacity, and we will study options to accelerate this timing,"" NCOC managing director Bruno Jardin said in a statement on Monday."
Exxon,2017-11,"In October, Kashagan's output fell to 182,000 barrels per day (23,000 tonnes per day) from 200,000 barrels per day in September, its highest monthly output figure, sources said."
Exxon,2017-11,"It was the first biggest fall in production since May this year and comes at time when NCOC delayed plans to ramp up output to 370,000 bpd from the end of 2017. [nL8N1N74OD]"
Exxon,2017-11,"""Production is not really stable. It's difficult to forecast anything,"" a source close to one of Kashagan consortium shareholders said."
Exxon,2017-11,"""... with the start of gas re-injection in August this year we have learned a great deal about how the reservoir reacts. Pressure decline, and hence production increase, is going to be more gradual than we originally anticipated,"" Bruno said."
Exxon,2017-11,"Kashagan's output will only rise above 200,000 barrels per day if gas re-injection goes well, industry sources familiar with the oilfield development said."
Exxon,2017-11,"All associated natural gas produced at Kashagan along with crude oil has to be utilised and should not be flared up for environmental and technical reasons. Gas produced has a high mercaptan content, which makes it pungent-smelling."
Exxon,2017-11,"""If they don't find a way to utilise the gas Kashagan will face the gas glut,"" an industry source said."
Exxon,2017-11,"Kashagan tentatively launched production in September 2013, but was forced to suspend it due to gas leaks blamed on faulty pipes. Production was restarted again last year."
Exxon,2017-11,The early development was fraught with delays and cost overruns that have brought total spending on the project to about $55 billion.
Exxon,2017-11,"The Kashagan consortium includes Kazakh state oil firm KazMunayGaz , Eni , ExxonMobil , Royal Dutch Shell , Total , China's CNPC [CNPET.UL] and Japan's Inpex <1605.T>."
Exxon,2017-11,"Kashagan to reach 370,000 bpd capacity more slowly than anticipated - NCOC - Reuters News"
Exxon,2017-11,"{{20171113T124005.055+0000}}Kashagan to reach 370,000 bpd capacity more slowly than anticipated - NCOCMOSCOW, Nov 13 (Reuters) - Kazakhstan's giant Kashagan oil field will reach its design capacity of 370,000 barrels per day more slowly than anticipated, its developer, the North Caspian Operating Company (NCOC), said on Monday."
Exxon,2017-11,"NCOC managing director Bruno Jardin said in a statement that the company was dedicated to reaching the design capacity of 370,000 barrels per day as soon as possible."
Exxon,2017-11,"""I expect that we will need year 2018 to fully accomplish this capacity, and we will study options to accelerate this timing,"" he said."
Exxon,2017-11,Pakistan expects no more big firms to exit LNG projects -minister - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-11,"{{20171113T073000.210+0000}}Pakistan expects no more big firms to exit LNG projects -ministerABU DHABI, Nov 13 (Reuters) - The oil market is rebalancing at an accelerating pace, as global levels of oil inventories have fallen visibly and demand for oil is roubust, OPEC Secretary-General Mohammad Barkindo said on Monday."
Exxon,2017-11,"Speaking at an energy industry conference, Barkindo said he was confident that both the oil industry and the global economy were benefitting from the deal to cut output among major producers."
Exxon,2017-11,"ABU DHABI, Nov 13 (Reuters) - Pakistan does not anticipate any more major companies will pull out of the liquefied natural gas (LNG) projects after the exit of Exxon Mobil , a state minister said on the sidelines of an Abu Dhabi energy conference."
Exxon,2017-11,"""The reason for that consortium to pull out can be within their own financial aspects that would be their own decision,"" said Jam Kamal Khan, the country's minister of state for petroleum."
Exxon,2017-11,"""We don't expect any more to pull out in fact investments are increasing."""
Exxon,2017-11,"Exxon Mobil has pulled out of a major project in Pakistan, in a potential blow to plans to boost imports of LNG after years of winter shortages."
Exxon,2017-11,"Differences among the six-member group behind the project in Port Qasim in Karachi mean other companies may also quit and join a rival scheme, Reuters reported last month, citing government officials and industry sources. [nL8N1N546H]"

Exxon,2017-11,{{20171110T183702.747+0000}}BUZZ-Oil stocks down on higher U.S. output forecast** Oil prices fell on forecasts that U.S. shale production will continue to grow as prices hold near 28-month highs

Exxon,2017-11,"{{20171109T222152.796+0000}}UPDATE 1-Exxon Baton Rouge large CDU may return to production next week -sources(Adds company no-comment, details on units, outage)"
Exxon,2017-11,"HOUSTON, Nov 9 (Reuters) - ExxonMobil Corp may return the large crude distillation unit (CDU) and a coker at its 502,500 barrel-per-day (bpd) Baton Rouge, Louisiana, refinery by the middle of next week, sources familiar with plant operations said on Thursday."
Exxon,2017-11,"The 210,000 bpd CDU was taken out of production after a fire heavily damaged the 75,000-bpd reformer on Nov. 1, the sources said. The 32,000 bpd coking unit was shut on Tuesday."
Exxon,2017-11,The CDU is the largest of four at the refinery. CDUs do the primary refining of crude oil and provide hydrocarbon feedstock for all other units.
Exxon,2017-11,"The coker was shut in preparation for the CDU's restart. There are three cokers at the refinery that convert residual crude oil from distillation units into either feedstock for motor fuels or petroleum coke, a substitute for coal."
Exxon,2017-11,"The reformer was heavily damaged in the fire and remains shut, the sources said."
Exxon,2017-11,"{{20171109T215529.952+0000}}Exxon Baton Rouge large CDU may return to production next week -sourcesHOUSTON, Nov 9 (Reuters) - ExxonMobil Corp may return the large crude distillation unit (CDU) and a coker at its 502,500 barrel-per-day (bpd) Baton Rouge, Louisiana, refinery by the middle of next week, sources familiar with plant operations said on Thursday."
Exxon,2017-11,"The 210,000 bpd CDU was taken out of production after a fire heavily damaged the 75,000-bpd reformer on Nov. 1, the sources said. The 32,000 bpd coking unit was shut on Tuesday."
Exxon,2017-11,BREAKINGVIEWS-Even China can't thaw Alaska's LNG ice age - Reuters Breakingviews
Exxon,2017-11,{{20171109T175233.073+0000}}BREAKINGVIEWS-Even China can't thaw Alaska's LNG ice age(The author is a Reuters Breakingviews columnist. The opinions expressed are her own.)
Exxon,2017-11,"DALLAS, Nov 9 (Reuters Breakingviews) - Alaska's liquefied natural gas projects are in an ice age that even China's riches won't thaw. The U.S. state has been trying to tap its considerable resource since the 1970s. Exxon Mobil and BP walked away from projects last year because the costly endeavor doesn't compute at current prices. China's cheap debt and need for gas alter the equation, but other energy sources still look better than the Last Frontier."
Exxon,2017-11,"While Alaska's lands are resource-rich, they're so remote that infrastructure is hard to build. The Prudhoe Bay region has produced some 17 billion barrels of oil since its discovery, according to the Resource Development Council of Alaska. But much of what was pulled out has been pumped back in because it has nowhere to go."
Exxon,2017-11,"China, seizing the moment of President Donald Trump's trip to Beijing, is now offering to invest in the project which requires new plants along with 800 miles of pipe. It is undeterred by a report by Wood Mackenzie, a consultant for the oil majors, which last year said oil prices would have to be above $70 a barrel before an investor could ink the kind of 12 percent return most global oil producers target."
Exxon,2017-11,"A few things are different for the People's Republic. Even though oil is still below $70, Chinese state oil companies like Sinopec have access to cheap debt, and might accept a lower return in exchange for securing a patch of liquefied natural gas. China's shift from coal means that gas demand is set to rise 8.7 percent per year through 2022, according to the International Energy Agency."
Exxon,2017-11,"- The state of Alaska signed a joint development agreement with China Petrochemical, CIC [CIC.UL] and the Bank of China <601988.SS> to develop the state's liquefied natural gas resources."
Exxon,2017-11,"- The agreement, signed in the presence of U.S. President Donald Trump and Chinese President Xi Jinping, would include several processing plants and an 800-mile pipeline."
Exxon,2017-11,"- BP and Exxon walked away from the project last year after Wood Mackenzie, a consultant to the firms, said the project would produce 12 percent returns only if oil prices hit $70 a barrel."
Exxon,2017-11,"- For previous columns by the author, Reuters customers can click on [SILVA/]"
Exxon,2017-11,"After years of famine, oil dividends back on menu - Reuters News"
Exxon,2017-11,"{{20171109T152224.430+0000}}After years of famine, oil dividends back on menu(Fixes last bullet point to say .. majors' ..not.. major's)"
Exxon,2017-11,* Majors seek to show they can make profit in low oil prices
Exxon,2017-11,"LONDON, Nov 9 (Reuters) - The world's top oil and gas companies are under growing pressure to revive share and dividend rewards to investors as profits and oil prices get back on track after a three-year crunch."
Exxon,2017-11,"BP fired the opening shot last week by surprising the market with the resumption of share buybacks after diluting share value for three years through scrip dividends, where investors can opt to receive dividends in shares or cash.[nL8N1N61IG]"
Exxon,2017-11,"The pressure is now on Royal Dutch Shell to make good on commitments made in 2015, following the decision to acquire BG Group for $54 billion, to remove scrip in 2017 and launch a $25 billion share buyback programme from 2017 to 2020."
Exxon,2017-11,"""There is a competition to see who can first remove the scrip, resume the buyback and then maybe, how much can you buy back and compensate for years of share dilution,"" said Jags Walia, asset manager at Dutch pension fund APG, which holds shares in Shell and BP."
Exxon,2017-11,"""I'd like to see them (Shell) announce the turning off of scrip, start talking about the $25 billion buyback - it has been a while since they spoke about that."""
Exxon,2017-11,"Shell did not provide an update on its plans with its third-quarter results, which showed the company generated sufficient cash to cover dividends for the fifth straight quarter, outdoing its larger rival Exxon Mobil . [nL8N1N81KV]"
Exxon,2017-11,"Chief Financial Officer Jessica Uhl said in a call last week that Shell's priorities remain to reduce debt, pay dividends and turn off scrip before turning to share repurchases."
Exxon,2017-11,"Changing the dividend policy will have a significant impact on Shell's balance sheet even with cashflow soaring to $28 billion in the first nine months. Dividend payouts for the Anglo-Dutch company in the 12 months to September amounted to $15 billion, with scrip accounting for around a quarter."
Exxon,2017-11,"Norway's Statoil confirmed in October it would revert to full cash dividends from the fourth quarter, after ending a two-year scrip dividend programme.[nL8N1N10QO]"
Exxon,2017-11,France's Total said it will scrap the discount offered for scrip shares in 2018.
Exxon,2017-11,"Shares of oil companies went through a roller coaster in recent years, tracking the collapse of oil prices in 2014 from over $100 a barrel to as low as $28 a barrel."
Exxon,2017-11,"Deep cost savings, job cuts, asset sales and the recovery in oil prices to above $64 a barrel this month have all helped boost profits and shares back to levels similar to 2014."
Exxon,2017-11,"With the Shell's $30 billion asset disposal programme on track to be completed almost a year ahead of schedule and debt trending towards around 20 percent, removing scrip will be in focus at its investor day at the end of the month."
Exxon,2017-11,"""The pressure is on Shell to draw a line in the sand and commit to end scrip dividend,"" said Brendan Warn, analyst at BMO Capital Markets."
Exxon,2017-11,"Removing scrip, effectively used to preserve cash in hard times, will send the clearest message yet that Shell, as well as other companies, have adapted to a world of lower prices, Warn said."
Exxon,2017-11,"Dividends are a major burden on oil majors' balance sheets, amounting to more than $47 billion in 2017."
Exxon,2017-11,"But none, bar Italy's Eni cut levels throughout the three-year downturn. Shell has repeatedly boasted that it hasn't reduced dividends since the Second World War."
Exxon,2017-11,Scrip and suspending buybacks were still vital for many companies to survive at crude prices of around $50 a barrel in 2017.
Exxon,2017-11,"HSBC estimates that BP's operations will fully cover $8 billion of dividend payments as well as $16 billion in spending at $59 a barrel this year, going down to $53 a barrel in 2018 when excluding payments for the 2010 Deepwater Horizon spill."
Exxon,2017-11,"For Shell, scrip has helped reduce the breakeven price in 2017 from $55 a barrel to $50 a barrel, according to HSBC."
Exxon,2017-11,Exxon slowed down last year its massive share repurchase programme as earnings dropped. It nevertheless kept with its 35-year-old tradition of raising dividends.
Exxon,2017-11,"Chevron held off on a dividend raise for the fourth quarter due to market uncertainty, but in July it said such a move would be its first use of cash."

Exxon,2017-11,"** Given ETF sector weightings, growth/value tug-of-war has been coming down to tech vs financials two-horse race"
Exxon,2017-11,"** Tech, IVW heaviest weighting (38 pct of value), financials IVE's greatest weighting (28 pct)"
Exxon,2017-11,** IVW also includes significant health care and cons disc exposure (both 16 pct)
Exxon,2017-11,"** Behind fins in IVE, next is health care (12 pct), and energy (11 pct)"
Exxon,2017-11,** Tech and financials top two S&P 500 <.SPX> sectors since Trump's election: tech up 40 pct vs fins 31 pct [nL1N1NC0RZ]
Exxon,2017-11,"** However, despite an initial post-election ratio slide (value had upper hand), more recent action shows growth's strong outperformance [nL1N1NC102] [nL2N1N70N5]"
Exxon,2017-11,"** Indeed, tech up 38 pct YTD vs fins 13 pct, and tech up 10 pct QTD vs fins just 2 pct [nL1N1NC0LQ] [nL3N1NE5HE] [nL2N1MF1EJ]"

Exxon,2017-11,"** That said, tech potentially overowned, now 25 pct of total SPX market value; fins ~14 pct"

Exxon,2017-11,"{{20171108T192036.640+0000}}UPDATE 2-Exxon Baton Rouge refinery CDU, coker may restart next week -sources(Adds company no comment)"
Exxon,2017-11,"HOUSTON, Nov 8 (Reuters) - ExxonMobil Corp plans to restart the 210,000 barrel-per-day (bpd) crude distillation unit (CDU) at its 502,500 bpd Baton Rouge, Louisiana, refinery early next week, sources familiar with plant operations said on Wednesday."
Exxon,2017-11,"A 32,000 bpd coking unit at the refinery, shut on Tuesday, may restart over the weekend, the sources said."
Exxon,2017-11,"The CDU was taken out of production after a fire heavily damaged the 75,000-bpd reformer on Nov. 1, the sources said. The unit is the largest of four at the refinery that do the primary refining of crude oil and provide hydrocarbon feedstock for all other units."
Exxon,2017-11,"The crude unit was to be brought back on-line later on Nov. 1, but instead was kept down for planned work."
Exxon,2017-11,"The coker shutdown was also planned, the sources said. Cokers convert residual crude oil into either feedstock for motor fuels or petroleum coke, a substitute for coal."
Exxon,2017-11,"{{20171108T180251.267+0000}}Exxon Baton Rouge refinery coker, large CDU shut -sourcesHOUSTON, Nov 8 (Reuters) - The large crude distillation unit (CDU) and a coker are shut at ExxonMobil Corp's 502,500 barrel-per-day (bpd) Baton Rouge, Louisiana, refinery on Wednesday, said sources familiar with plant operations."
Exxon,2017-11,"The 210,000-bpd CDU is expected to restart early next week, the sources said."
Exxon,2017-11,RPT-INSIGHT-Peak oil? Majors aren't buying into the threat from renewables - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-11,{{20171108T120002.956+0000}}RPT-INSIGHT-Peak oil? Majors aren't buying into the threat from renewables(Repeats for additional clients with no changes to text)
Exxon,2017-11,"HOUSTON/LONDON, Nov 8 (Reuters) - Two decades ago, BP set out to transcend oil, adopting a sunburst logo to convey its plans to pour $8 billion over a decade into renewable technologies, even promising to power its gas stations with the sun."
Exxon,2017-11,"That transformation - marketed as ""Beyond Petroleum"" - led to manufacturing solar panels in Australia, Spain and the United States and erecting wind farms in the United States and the Netherlands."
Exxon,2017-11,"Today, BP might be more aptly branded ""Back to Petroleum"" after exiting or scaling back its renewable energy investments. Lower-cost Chinese components upended its solar panel business, which the firm shed in 2011. A year later, BP tried to sell its U.S. wind power business but couldn't get a buyer."
Exxon,2017-11,"""We made very big bets in the past,"" BP Chief Executive Bob Dudley told Reuters in an interview. ""A lot of those didn't work. We're not sure yet what will be commercially acceptable."""
Exxon,2017-11,The costly lesson of the biggest foray yet by an oil major into renewable energy was not lost on rival firms.
Exxon,2017-11,Even as governments and environmentalists forecast a peak in oil demand within a generation - and China and India say they may eventually ban gasoline and diesel vehicles - leaders of the world's biggest oil firms are not buying the argument that their traditional business faces any imminent threat.
Exxon,2017-11,"A Reuters analysis of clean energy investments and forecasts by oil majors, along with exclusive interviews with top oil executives, reveal mostly token investments in alternative energy. Today, renewable power projects get about 3 percent of $100 billion in combined annual spending by the five biggest oil firms, according to energy consultancy Wood Mackenzie."
Exxon,2017-11,"BP, Chevron , Exxon Mobil , Royal Dutch Shell and Total are instead milking their drilling and processing assets to finance investor payouts now and bolster balance sheets for the future. They believe they can enter new energy sectors later by acquiring companies or technologies if and when others prove them profitable."
Exxon,2017-11,"""There is no sign of peak demand right now,"" said Chevron CEO John Watson, an economist by training, who is retiring in early 2018. ""For the next 10 or 20 years, we expect to see oil demand growth."""
Exxon,2017-11,"The International Energy Agency forecasts a 10 percent rise in oil demand through 2040, reflecting the consensus among oil firms. The earliest estimate for peak oil demand from any oil company is late next decade, by Shell CEO Ben van Beurden."
Exxon,2017-11,"History shows energy transitions - from wood to coal to oil - take a long time. Coal's contribution to world energy consumption peaked recently at 28 percent and remains above the share from natural gas, though just below oil's one-third."
Exxon,2017-11,"Profit, if any, from the majors' decades-long interest in renewable energy ventures is unclear. None of the largest oil companies disclose earnings from their solar, wind or biofuels ventures."
Exxon,2017-11,"Investors such as Alasdair McKinnon, portfolio manager at Scottish Investment Trust, believe oil will sustain shareholders far into the future."
Exxon,2017-11,"""There isn't a viable alternative to fossil fuels on the horizon,"" he said. ""We're not buying into the long-term demand destruction for oil."""
Exxon,2017-11,"The confidence in oil's future relies largely on rising consumption from emerging economies. Exxon forecasts that transportation will require 25 percent more fuel by 2040, propelled by growth in Asia. Chevron's analysis of the India and Nigeria markets, meanwhile, concludes that infrastructure needed for electric cars is unlikely to be built."
Exxon,2017-11,"Cars account for about a fifth of oil consumption, BP estimates. So if electric vehicles do eventually capture mass markets, oil firms would still expect growing demand from the air, rail and trucking industries."
Exxon,2017-11,"Natural gas - now a smaller business than oil for most majors - can grow to nearly a quarter of all energy used by displacing coal in power generation and through expanded uses in chemicals, these companies forecast. Natural gas can also fuel the power needed for electric cars."
Exxon,2017-11,"Although Shell forecasts peak oil demand coming earlier than its rivals, it is preparing for that prospect mostly with massive natural gas investments. The firm last year spent $54 billion acquiring BG Group, which derives half its production from gas. Chevron, Exxon and Shell recently have spent billions of dollars on new liquefied natural gas projects across the globe."
Exxon,2017-11,"Critics of oil majors' cautious renewable strategy - including some big investors - say the firms are being short-sighted in their trust that change will come slow, or that one fossil fuel will gradually replace another. Just as cheap natural gas is supplanting coal, even cheaper wind or solar eventually will displace gas, they argue."
Exxon,2017-11,"South Australia is soon to become a proving ground for a project could pave the way for renewable power to supplant fossil fuels for peak electricity - a combined wind farm and grid-scale battery storage facility, by electric-car maker Tesla Inc and operator Windlab Ltd."
Exxon,2017-11,"Fossil fuel companies need to quickly reorient themselves to the low returns of the solar and wind industries, said Jules Kortenhorst, a former Shell executive who runs the Rocky Mountain Institute, a nonprofit energy research organization."
Exxon,2017-11,"""You cannot flip a switch on a Monday morning from being one to another,"" he said. ""Paychecks in the oil and gas industry are based on fundamentally believing that the world cannot see economic growth without fossil fuels."""
Exxon,2017-11,"To achieve the same share of the renewables market that the largest publicly-traded oil companies now hold in oil and gas would require an investment of about $350 billion over the next 18 years, estimates Wood Mackenzie. Such spending would cut into the generous dividends that oil firms' shareholders have come to expect."
Exxon,2017-11,"""We think it will be a real challenge for these companies to change their business model,"" said Nathan Fabian, director of policy at Principles for Responsible Investment (PRI), a United Nations-backed group."
Exxon,2017-11,"PRI has guidelines calling for investment analysis that weighs environmental, social and governance issues. Its principles have been adopted by investors with $70 trillion in assets under management."
Exxon,2017-11,"Oil companies have made relatively modest investments a wide range of renewable technologies. Chevron has a smattering of mostly small wind and solar ventures; Shell invests in sugar-cane ethanol in South America, wind farms in the United States and electric-car charging stations in Europe; and BP still owns the U.S. wind farms it once tried to sell."
Exxon,2017-11,John Browne - who as BP's CEO two decades ago helped launch the early investments in renewables - said he still believes the renewable power will grow.
Exxon,2017-11,"""It will take time,"" he said in an interview with Reuters last month. ""And they have time."""
Exxon,2017-11,"Shell pledged to invest up to $1 billion a year by 2020 in what it calls ""new energies."""
Exxon,2017-11,"Total said this year it would spend $500 million annually on developing alternatives. But soon after that announcement, it unveiled its $7.5 billion acquisition of Maersk Oil, part of a plan to pump more crude from Norway's North Sea."
Exxon,2017-11,Total CEO Patrick Pouyanne in October explained the focus on economics at an October oil conference in London.
Exxon,2017-11,"""When you ask our customers what their priority is, either in developed economies or in emerging countries, price comes first,"" he said. A hasty shift to renewables, he said, ""could bring great economic and social damage to our 6 billion customers."""
Exxon,2017-11,"Exxon Mobil is backing research into biofuels, joining with gene modification firm Synthetic Genomics to coax algae to produce more lipids, an oil substitute. It hasn't detailed its investment but said the effort remains far from commercialization. By comparison, Exxon this year spent $5.6 billion on U.S. shale oil assets."
Exxon,2017-11,"Some of the oil industry's largest customers are planning a shift to renewable alternatives, especially in transportation, which accounts for about a quarter of annual energy consumption."
Exxon,2017-11,"Ford Motor Co earlier this fall disclosed it would aim, by 2030, to derive a third of its sales from battery-powered cars and another third from gas-electric hybrids. [nL4N1ME3GX]"
Exxon,2017-11,"A startup backed by Boeing Co and JetBlue Airways Corp recently announced plans for a small hybrid jet by 2022, using batteries from Tesla and battery supplier Panasonic Corp <6752.T>. [nL2N1MG1HZ]"
Exxon,2017-11,Yet oil firms continue to forecast aggressive growth in liquid fuels. Exxon predicts 90 percent of the transportation industry will rely on petroleum through 2040.
Exxon,2017-11,"BP projects the world's auto fleet doubling to 1.8 billion vehicles by 2035, with only 75 million of those powered by electricity."
Exxon,2017-11,"""We'll see if (electric cars) can be delivered in a way that doesn't require large subsidies"" from governments, Chevron's Watson told Reuters. ""That's what we're seeing now."""
Exxon,2017-11,INSIGHT-Peak oil? Majors aren't buying into the threat from renewables - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-11,{{20171108T060002.732+0000}}INSIGHT-Peak oil? Majors aren't buying into the threat from renewablesBy Ernest Scheyder and Ron Bousso
Exxon,2017-11,"HOUSTON/LONDON, Nov 8 (Reuters) - Two decades ago, BP set out to transcend oil, adopting a sunburst logo to convey its plans to pour $8 billion over a decade into renewable technologies, even promising to power its gas stations with the sun."

Today, renewable power projects get about 3 percent of $100 billion in combined annual spending by the five biggest oil firms, according to energy consultancy Wood Mackenzie."
Exxon,2017-11,"BP, Chevron , Exxon Mobil , Royal Dutch Shell and Total are instead milking their drilling and processing assets to finance investor payouts now and bolster balance sheets for the future. They believe they can enter new energy sectors later by acquiring companies or technologies if and when others prove them profitable."
Exxon,2017-11,"""There is no sign of peak demand right now,"" said Chevron CEO John Watson, an economist by training, who is retiring in early 2018. ""For the next 10 or 20 years, we expect to see oil demand growth."""
Exxon,2017-11,"The International Energy Agency forecasts a 10 percent rise in oil demand through 2040, reflecting the consensus among oil firms. The earliest estimate for peak oil demand from any oil company is late next decade, by Shell CEO Ben van Beurden."
Exxon,2017-11,"History shows energy transitions - from wood to coal to oil - take a long time. Coal's contribution to world energy consumption peaked recently at 28 percent and remains above the share from natural gas, though just below oil's one-third."
Exxon,2017-11,"Profit, if any, from the majors' decades-long interest in renewable energy ventures is unclear. None of the largest oil companies disclose earnings from their solar, wind or biofuels ventures."
Exxon,2017-11,"Investors such as Alasdair McKinnon, portfolio manager at Scottish Investment Trust, believe oil will sustain shareholders far into the future."
Exxon,2017-11,"""There isn't a viable alternative to fossil fuels on the horizon,"" he said. ""We're not buying into the long-term demand destruction for oil."""

Exxon forecasts that transportation will require 25 percent more fuel by 2040, propelled by growth in Asia. Chevron's analysis of the India and Nigeria markets, meanwhile, concludes that infrastructure needed for electric cars is unlikely to be built."

Just as cheap natural gas is supplanting coal, even cheaper wind or solar eventually will displace gas, they argue."
Exxon,2017-11,"South Australia is soon to become a proving ground for a project could pave the way for renewable power to supplant fossil fuels for peak electricity - a combined wind farm and grid-scale battery storage facility, by electric-car maker Tesla Inc and operator Windlab Ltd."
Exxon,2017-11,"Fossil fuel companies need to quickly reorient themselves to the low returns of the solar and wind industries, said Jules Kortenhorst, a former Shell executive who runs the Rocky Mountain Institute, a nonprofit energy research organization."
Exxon,2017-11,"""You cannot flip a switch on a Monday morning from being one to another,"" he said. ""Paychecks in the oil and gas industry are based on fundamentally believing that the world cannot see economic growth without fossil fuels."""
Exxon,2017-11,"To achieve the same share of the renewables market that the largest publicly-traded oil companies now hold in oil and gas would require an investment of about $350 billion over the next 18 years, estimates consultancy Wood Mackenzie. Such spending would cut into the generous dividends that oil firms' shareholders have come to expect."
Exxon,2017-11,"""We think it will be a real challenge for these companies to change their business model,"" said Nathan Fabian, director of policy at Principles for Responsible Investment (PRI), a United Nations-backed group."
Exxon,2017-11,"PRI has guidelines calling for investment analysis that weighs environmental, social and governance issues. Its principles have been adopted by investors with $70 trillion in assets under management."
Exxon,2017-11,"Oil companies have made relatively modest investments a wide range of renewable technologies. Chevron has a smattering of mostly small wind and solar ventures; Shell invests in sugar-cane ethanol in South America, wind farms in the United States and electric-car charging stations in Europe; and BP still owns the U.S. wind farms it once tried to sell."
Exxon,2017-11,John Browne - who as BP's CEO two decades ago helped launch the early investments in renewables - said he still believes the renewable power will grow.
Exxon,2017-11,"""It will take time,"" he said in an interview with Reuters last month. ""And they have time."""
Exxon,2017-11,"Shell pledged to invest up to $1 billion a year by 2020 in what it calls ""new energies."""
Exxon,2017-11,"Total said this year it would spend $500 million annually on developing alternatives. But soon after that announcement, it unveiled its $7.5 billion acquisition of Maersk Oil, part of a plan to pump more crude from Norway's North Sea."
Exxon,2017-11,Total CEO Patrick Pouyanne in October explained the focus on economics at an October oil conference in London.
Exxon,2017-11,"""When you ask our customers what their priority is, either in developed economies or in emerging countries, price comes first,"" he said. A hasty shift to renewables, he said, ""could bring great economic and social damage to our 6 billion customers."""
Exxon,2017-11,"Exxon Mobil is backing research into biofuels, joining with gene modification firm Synthetic Genomics to coax algae to produce more lipids, an oil substitute. It hasn't detailed its investment but said the effort remains far from commercialization. By comparison, Exxon this year spent $5.6 billion on U.S. shale oil assets."
Exxon,2017-11,"Some of the oil industry's largest customers are planning a shift to renewable alternatives, especially in transportation, which accounts for about a quarter of annual energy consumption."
Exxon,2017-11,"Ford Motor Co earlier this fall disclosed it would aim, by 2030, to derive a third of its sales from battery-powered cars and another third from gas-electric hybrids. [nL4N1ME3GX]"
Exxon,2017-11,"A startup backed by Boeing Co and JetBlue Airways Corp recently announced plans for a small hybrid jet by 2022, using batteries from Tesla and battery supplier Panasonic Corp <6752.T>. [nL2N1MG1HZ]"
Exxon,2017-11,Yet oil firms continue to forecast aggressive growth in liquid fuels. Exxon predicts 90 percent of the transportation industry will rely on petroleum through 2040.
Exxon,2017-11,"BP projects the world's auto fleet doubling to 1.8 billion vehicles by 2035, with only 75 million of those powered by electricity."
Exxon,2017-11,"""We'll see if (electric cars) can be delivered in a way that doesn't require large subsidies"" from governments, Chevron's Watson told Reuters. ""That's what we're seeing now."""

Exxon,2017-11,"{{20171108T000000.000+0000}}RPT-INSIGHT-Peak oil? Majors aren't buying into the threat from renewablesHOUSTON/LONDON, Nov 8 (Reuters)"
Exxon,2017-11,"HOUSTON/LONDON, Nov 8 (Reuters) - Two decades ago, BP set out to transcend oil, adopting a sunburst logo to convey its plans to pour $8 billion over a decade into renewable technologies, even promising to power its gas stations with the sun."
Exxon,2017-11,"That transformation - marketed as ""Beyond Petroleum"" - led to manufacturing solar panels in Australia, Spain and the United States and erecting wind farms in the United States and the Netherlands."
Exxon,2017-11,"Today, BP might be more aptly branded ""Back to Petroleum"" after exiting or scaling back its renewable energy investments. Lower-cost Chinese components upended its solar panel business, which the firm shed in 2011. A year later, BP tried to sell its U.S. wind power business but couldn't get a buyer."
Exxon,2017-11,"""We made very big bets in the past,"" BP Chief Executive Bob Dudley told Reuters in an interview. ""A lot of those didn't work. We're not sure yet what will be commercially acceptable."""
Exxon,2017-11,The costly lesson of the biggest foray yet by an oil major into renewable energy was not lost on rival firms.
Exxon,2017-11,Even as governments and environmentalists forecast a peak in oil demand within a generation - and China and India say they may eventually ban gasoline and diesel vehicles - leaders of the world's biggest oil firms are not buying the argument that their traditional business faces any imminent threat.
Exxon,2017-11,"A Reuters analysis of clean energy investments and forecasts by oil majors, along with exclusive interviews with top oil executives, reveal mostly token investments in alternative energy. Today, renewable power projects get about 3 percent of $100 billion in combined annual spending by the five biggest oil firms, according to energy consultancy Wood Mackenzie."
Exxon,2017-11,"BP, Chevron , Exxon Mobil , Royal Dutch Shell and Total are instead milking their drilling and processing assets to finance investor payouts now and bolster balance sheets for the future. They believe they can enter new energy sectors later by acquiring companies or technologies if and when others prove them profitable."
Exxon,2017-11,"""There is no sign of peak demand right now,"" said Chevron CEO John Watson, an economist by training, who is retiring in early 2018. ""For the next 10 or 20 years, we expect to see oil demand growth."""
Exxon,2017-11,"The International Energy Agency forecasts a 10 percent rise in oil demand through 2040, reflecting the consensus among oil firms. The earliest estimate for peak oil demand from any oil company is late next decade, by Shell CEO Ben van Beurden."
Exxon,2017-11,"History shows energy transitions - from wood to coal to oil - take a long time. Coal's contribution to world energy consumption peaked recently at 28 percent and remains above the share from natural gas, though just below oil's one-third."
Exxon,2017-11,"Profit, if any, from the majors' decades-long interest in renewable energy ventures is unclear. None of the largest oil companies disclose earnings from their solar, wind or biofuels ventures."
Exxon,2017-11,"Investors such as Alasdair McKinnon, portfolio manager at Scottish Investment Trust, believe oil will sustain shareholders far into the future."
Exxon,2017-11,"""There isn't a viable alternative to fossil fuels on the horizon,"" he said. ""We're not buying into the long-term demand destruction for oil."""
Exxon,2017-11,"The confidence in oil's future relies largely on rising consumption from emerging economies. Exxon forecasts that transportation will require 25 percent more fuel by 2040, propelled by growth in Asia. Chevron's analysis of the India and Nigeria markets, meanwhile, concludes that infrastructure needed for electric cars is unlikely to be built."
Exxon,2017-11,"Cars account for about a fifth of oil consumption, BP estimates. So if electric vehicles do eventually capture mass markets, oil firms would still expect growing demand from the air, rail and trucking industries."
Exxon,2017-11,"Natural gas - now a smaller business than oil for most majors - can grow to nearly a quarter of all energy used by displacing coal in power generation and through expanded uses in chemicals, these companies forecast. Natural gas can also fuel the power needed for electric cars."
Exxon,2017-11,"Although Shell forecasts peak oil demand coming earlier than its rivals, it is preparing for that prospect mostly with massive natural gas investments. The firm last year spent $54 billion acquiring BG Group, which derives half its production from gas. Chevron, Exxon and Shell recently have spent billions of dollars on new liquefied natural gas projects across the globe."
Exxon,2017-11,"Critics of oil majors' cautious renewable strategy - including some big investors - say the firms are being short-sighted in their trust that change will come slow, or that one fossil fuel will gradually replace another. Just as cheap natural gas is supplanting coal, even cheaper wind or solar eventually will displace gas, they argue."
Exxon,2017-11,"South Australia is soon to become a proving ground for a project could pave the way for renewable power to supplant fossil fuels for peak electricity - a combined wind farm and grid-scale battery storage facility, by electric-car maker Tesla Inc and operator Windlab Ltd."
Exxon,2017-11,"Fossil fuel companies need to quickly reorient themselves to the low returns of the solar and wind industries, said Jules Kortenhorst, a former Shell executive who runs the Rocky Mountain Institute, a nonprofit energy research organization."
Exxon,2017-11,"""You cannot flip a switch on a Monday morning from being one to another,"" he said. ""Paychecks in the oil and gas industry are based on fundamentally believing that the world cannot see economic growth without fossil fuels."""
Exxon,2017-11,"To achieve the same share of the renewables market that the largest publicly-traded oil companies now hold in oil and gas would require an investment of about $350 billion over the next 18 years, estimates Wood Mackenzie. Such spending would cut into the generous dividends that oil firms' shareholders have come to expect."
Exxon,2017-11,"""We think it will be a real challenge for these companies to change their business model,"" said Nathan Fabian, director of policy at Principles for Responsible Investment (PRI), a United Nations-backed group."
Exxon,2017-11,"PRI has guidelines calling for investment analysis that weighs environmental, social and governance issues. Its principles have been adopted by investors with $70 trillion in assets under management."
Exxon,2017-11,"Oil companies have made relatively modest investments a wide range of renewable technologies. Chevron has a smattering of mostly small wind and solar ventures; Shell invests in sugar-cane ethanol in South America, wind farms in the United States and electric-car charging stations in Europe; and BP still owns the U.S. wind farms it once tried to sell."
Exxon,2017-11,John Browne - who as BP's CEO two decades ago helped launch the early investments in renewables - said he still believes the renewable power will grow.
Exxon,2017-11,"""It will take time,"" he said in an interview with Reuters last month. ""And they have time."""
Exxon,2017-11,"Shell pledged to invest up to $1 billion a year by 2020 in what it calls ""new energies."""
Exxon,2017-11,"Total said this year it would spend $500 million annually on developing alternatives. But soon after that announcement, it unveiled its $7.5 billion acquisition of Maersk Oil, part of a plan to pump more crude from Norway's North Sea."
Exxon,2017-11,Total CEO Patrick Pouyanne in October explained the focus on economics at an October oil conference in London.
Exxon,2017-11,"""When you ask our customers what their priority is, either in developed economies or in emerging countries, price comes first,"" he said. A hasty shift to renewables, he said, ""could bring great economic and social damage to our 6 billion customers."""
Exxon,2017-11,"Exxon Mobil is backing research into biofuels, joining with gene modification firm Synthetic Genomics to coax algae to produce more lipids, an oil substitute. It hasn't detailed its investment but said the effort remains far from commercialization. By comparison, Exxon this year spent $5.6 billion on U.S. shale oil assets."
Exxon,2017-11,"Some of the oil industry's largest customers are planning a shift to renewable alternatives, especially in transportation, which accounts for about a quarter of annual energy consumption."
Exxon,2017-11,"Ford Motor Co earlier this fall disclosed it would aim, by 2030, to derive a third of its sales from battery-powered cars and another third from gas-electric hybrids. [nL4N1ME3GX]"
Exxon,2017-11,"A startup backed by Boeing Co and JetBlue Airways Corp recently announced plans for a small hybrid jet by 2022, using batteries from Tesla and battery supplier Panasonic Corp <6752.T>. [nL2N1MG1HZ]"
Exxon,2017-11,Yet oil firms continue to forecast aggressive growth in liquid fuels. Exxon predicts 90 percent of the transportation industry will rely on petroleum through 2040.
Exxon,2017-11,"BP projects the world's auto fleet doubling to 1.8 billion vehicles by 2035, with only 75 million of those powered by electricity."
Exxon,2017-11,"""We'll see if (electric cars) can be delivered in a way that doesn't require large subsidies"" from governments, Chevron's Watson told Reuters. ""That's what we're seeing now."""

Exxon,2017-11,Oil at $70/barrel already a reality for some as Asian premium bites - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-11,"{{20171107T095917.710+0000}}Oil at $70/barrel already a reality for some as Asian premium bites* Robust demand, limited supplies underpin spot premiums"
Exxon,2017-11,"SINGAPORE, Nov 7 (Reuters) - The rising demand for crude oil that can more easily produce transportation fuels when refined has some Australian and Malaysian producers boasting cargoes valued at close to $70 a barrel, a hefty premium to global benchmarks ."
Exxon,2017-11,"Malaysia's state oil company Petronas [PETR.UL] sold last week a December-loading Miri Light cargo at a premium of about $4.50 a barrel to dated Brent, equivalent to about $69 at the latest prices, according to multiple traders that participate in the Asian regional crude market."
Exxon,2017-11,"Australian Barrow Island and Cooper Basin crudes are now close to $70 a barrel currently, based on premiums for grades of about $1.50 a barrel to Malaysian benchmark grade Kimanis, said the traders. Kimanis itself is priced at a premium of about $4.40 a barrel to dated Brent, which was assessed at $64.07 a barrel on Monday by price reporting agency S&P Global Platts."
Exxon,2017-11,"""Prices of domestic Australian grades are even higher than MCO (Malaysian Crude Oil),"" an Asian trader said. ""That would make them the most expensive crudes in the world."""
Exxon,2017-11,"Demand for these grades is rising because of the short distances to Asian refineries, which prize the crude for their low sulphur content and higher yields of more valuable oil products such as diesel, the traders said."
Exxon,2017-11,"Demand for short-haul grades has increased after the Brent oil market structure flipped into backwardation, when prompt prices are more than later prices. That means the value of the crude drops over the course of the voyage."
Exxon,2017-11,"The refiners are willing to pay up for the Australian and Malaysian crudes rather than incur the additional time and cost of shipping Brent supplies from the North Sea, the traders said."
Exxon,2017-11,"Typically, Asia-Pacific grades are sold to refineries in Southeast Asia and Australia or New Zealand that have a preference for low-sulphur oil."
Exxon,2017-11,Values for these grades have risen because of their scarcity.
Exxon,2017-11,"Petronas and its partners Royal Dutch Shell , ConocoPhillips , Murphy Oil Corp , Pertamina [PERTM.UL] sell about 6 million barrels of Kimanis each month."
Exxon,2017-11,But volumes for other Malaysian grades such as Kikeh and Labuan have fallen as output declines at the mature fields.
Exxon,2017-11,"Australia's crude and condensate production has been below 300,000 barrels per day (bpd) since September 2016, data from the country's Department of the Environment and Energy showed. In August it was 279,000 bpd."
Exxon,2017-11,"Santos Ltd produces about 30,000 bpd of Cooper Basin crude in southern Australia, according to its website."
Exxon,2017-11,"Santos and its partners, Chevron Corp and Mobil Australia Resources Co, a unit of Exxon Mobil Corp , produces 5,000 bpd of Barrow Island in western Australia, according to Santos."
Exxon,2017-11,"Aramco oil reserves audit two-thirds complete, may not be finished in 2017 -sources - Reuters News"
Exxon,2017-11,"{{20171107T080001.051+0000}}Aramco oil reserves audit two-thirds complete, may not be finished in 2017 -sourcesBy Alex Lawler and Rania El Gamal"
Exxon,2017-11,"LONDON/DUBAI, Nov 7 (Reuters) - An audit of Saudi Aramco's [IPO-ARMO.SE] oil reserves is unlikely to be completed before the end of 2017 because of the huge scale of the task, sources familiar with the matter said, a later timeframe than previously indicated."
Exxon,2017-11,"The audit has so far confirmed the reserves figures earlier given by Saudi Arabia, the sources said, an important part of the state oil company's preparatory work for its planned initial public offering next year."
Exxon,2017-11,"Saudi Arabia's reserves of easily recoverable oil have long been considered the world's largest. But there have also been questions about their volume and quality, and the audit seeks to provide internationally recognised figures for investors."
Exxon,2017-11,"""It's a huge task,"" a source familiar with the matter said, commenting on the progress of the reserves audit. ""They are about two-thirds of the way through. It's all going well and smoothly - no surprises."""
Exxon,2017-11,"For nearly 30 years - despite rising production, large swings in oil prices and improved technology - Riyadh has annually reported the same number for reserves of 261 billion barrels, according to BP's statistical review."
Exxon,2017-11,"Dallas-based DeGolyer and MacNaughton, and Gaffney, Cline and Associates, part of Baker Hughes , are involved in the auditing, sources have said. Baker Hughes declined to comment on the progress of the work, while DeGolyer did not respond to a request for comment."
Exxon,2017-11,"Asked to comment, Aramco said: ""We do not comment on rumours and speculation. Investors will receive relevant information in due course in connection with the IPO."""
Exxon,2017-11,"An industry source had told Reuters in March that Aramco aimed to have one of the two reserves auditors wrap up the review this year, long before the planned listing. But this now looks unlikely. [nL5N1GL5AF]"
Exxon,2017-11,"""Aramco wants to make sure the companies are shown full data to avoid sceptical remarks on its reserves later on,"" a second source said. ""It's unlikely the audit will be finished this year."""
Exxon,2017-11,"A third source said auditing work on the major Aramco fields was completed, leaving smaller fields still to be audited."
Exxon,2017-11,A reserves total that is significantly above or below the 261 billion figure is likely to affect Aramco's potential value. Earlier phases of the audit have supported Aramco's statements on the total size of deposits. [nL5N1FH2YM]
Exxon,2017-11,"The sale of around 5 percent of Aramco next year is a centrepiece of Vision 2030, an ambitious reform plan to diversify the Saudi economy beyond oil which is championed by Saudi Arabia's Crown Prince Mohammad bin Salman."
Exxon,2017-11,"No decision about the location of the international share listing has been announced, fuelling market speculation the IPO could be delayed or shelved. But Prince Mohammad told Reuters in October it was still on track for 2018. [nL8N1N13YC]"

Exxon,2017-11,Shell looks beyond road fuels to secure future of refining - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-11,"{{20171106T070002.682+0000}}Shell looks beyond road fuels to secure future of refining* Asphalt, plastics, chemicals to sustain demand, Shell says"
Exxon,2017-11,"LONDON, Nov 6 (Reuters) - While the world braces for the electric-vehicle revolution, Royal Dutch Shell is betting on growing appetite for asphalt and plastics to sustain its century-old oil refining business for the coming decades."
Exxon,2017-11,"Converting crude oil into products ranging from gasoline to industrial chemicals has long faced obstacles due to volatile profits, high costs, safety issues and pollution and more recently, forecasts of peaking demand for oil."
Exxon,2017-11,"But refining, together with trading, marketing and chemicals - known together as downstream - has proved its importance during the oil industry's downturn since 2014, providing the bulk of Shell's profits as the price of crude collapsed."
Exxon,2017-11,"Shell has in recent years transformed its downstream business by selling some plants and upgrading others to have them better resist oil price fluctuations and shifts in demand, delivering double-digit returns on capital employed."
Exxon,2017-11,"""Refining will continue to be part of our portfolio for decades to come,"" said Shell's head of manufacturing Lori Ryerkerk, who is in charge of refining."
Exxon,2017-11,Shell is perhaps the most aggressive in its sector in forecasting that the demand for gasoline could reach an apex by the 2030s as drivers shift to electric vehicles and traditional engines become more efficient.
Exxon,2017-11,"But still, Shell says, the continued expansion of the world's economy, particularly in Asia, means consumption of other refined oil products and petrochemicals is likely to grow."
Exxon,2017-11,"For instance, there are no economically viable substitutes for asphalt, needed to build roads, or for the polymers and chemicals used to produce plastics for cars, toys and clothes, Ryerkerk said."
Exxon,2017-11,"The Anglo-Dutch company plans to double the size of its chemicals business by the middle of the next decade with several new plants including in Louisiana and Pennsylvania that benefit from access to cheap shale gas, said Shell's head of chemicals, Graham van't Hoff."
Exxon,2017-11,It also wants 20 percent of sales from its fuel stations worldwide to come from recharging electric vehicles and low-carbon fuels by 2025. [nL5N1LT4R6]
Exxon,2017-11,The oil sector's outlook for growth in demand for oil and plastics could prove wrong if governments around the world introduce regulations to reduce fossil fuel consumption in their fight against pollution and global warming. A study published last week said a quarter of the world's oil refineries risk closure by 2035 if those targets are met. [nL8N1N60XR]
Exxon,2017-11,"Just as some countries such as China and India contemplate banning gasoline and diesel vehicles, rules to limit consumption of plastics such as bottles and bags could dampen demand, analysts said."
Exxon,2017-11,"""Regulation is one of the biggest risks to the business,"" said Jason Kenney, head of European oil and gas equity research at Banco Santander."
Exxon,2017-11,Overcapacity is another danger as other companies including Exxon Mobil and France's Total also expand into petrochemicals.
Exxon,2017-11,"""Shell currently offers double-digit returns on capital employed from downstream and chemicals. But then you could have a flood of capacity and it will be a difficult sector to remain competitive for decades,"" Kenney said."
Exxon,2017-11,"Even when demand starts to fall, Shell says its refining arm will have an edge over many competitors thanks to the company's access to its own, cheaper crude and complex trading operations that curb its vulnerability to fluctuating oil prices."
Exxon,2017-11,"It has 43,000 petrol stations in 70 countries, making Shell the world's largest fuel retailer. Shell recently introduced battery charging spots at a number of stations in Britain and plans to develop hydrogen fuelling stations in Germany."
Exxon,2017-11,"Shell also supplies 11 percent of the world's lubricants needed in cars, trucks and heavy industrial machinery. It has one of the world's largest aviation fuel businesses, fuelling a plane every 40 seconds."
Exxon,2017-11,"""Downstream is a highly resilient business. It is pretty independent to changes in crude price,"" said John Abbott, head of Shell's downstream business."
Exxon,2017-11,"""We have a competitive edge going into the energy transition,"" Abbott said."
Exxon,2017-11,"Shell has interests in more than 20 refineries and processed around 2.6 million barrels of oil per day in 2016, while its 15 petrochemical plants processed 6.2 million tonnes last year."

Exxon,2017-11,BREAKINGVIEWS-Singapore's DBS gets closer to oil reality - Reuters Breakingviews
Exxon,2017-11,{{20171106T032548.091+0000}}BREAKINGVIEWS-Singapore's DBS gets closer to oil reality(The author is a Reuters Breakingviews columnist. The opinions expressed are her own.)
Exxon,2017-11,"SINGAPORE, Nov 6 (Reuters Breakingviews) - Singapore's DBS Group has taken a big dose of oil medicine. The $43 billion banking titan lifted net provisions in the latest quarter to a 15-year high. Like its two largest peers, Overseas-Chinese Banking Corp and United Overseas Bank , DBS reckons the worst of the shock in crude prices is over. The offshore industry is still aching, though, leaving both the economy and vessel valuations vulnerable. Local lenders may yet feel more pain."
Exxon,2017-11,"After a rough 18 months of watching Swiber Holdings and other providers of engineering and construction services reel into distress, there is some good news for Singapore's banks. Interest rates are set to gradually rise. The Lion City's property market is recovering, and its broader $300 billion economy is showing signs of improvement. Wealth management and transaction-banking businesses are gaining ground."
Exxon,2017-11,DBS's move on Monday to set aside another S$815 million ($597 million) for troubled loans is an effort to get investors to focus on that momentum. Provisions now cover about half its oil-and-gas services non-performing debt. Singapore's biggest bank also has aggressively written down the value of offshore service vessels used to secure many of the loans to 25 percent.
Exxon,2017-11,"That's a helpful step, especially if the remaining portfolio is as strong as DBS is arguing. It doesn't mean the worst is definitively past, however, despite a 31 percent run-up in its shares this year."
Exxon,2017-11,"After distress first hit roughly two years ago when oil tumbled below $50 a barrel, the industry is now experiencing something of a second wave as big producers and service providers come to terms with lower prices for longer. They make it harder to justify complex projects. Drilling cancellations in the region, such as Exxon Mobil's exit from East Natuna in Indonesia this summer, will persist. Halliburton said last month its clients were focused on ""cost-effective"" production."
Exxon,2017-11,"It's the sort of news that augurs poorly for banks, especially ones that have not pushed down energy-related collateral nearer to liquidation levels as DBS has. More loans also may wind up added to the endangered list. Singapore's three biggest banks are getting closer to the energy reality, but aren't necessarily fully there."
Exxon,2017-11,"- DBS, Singapore's biggest lender, on Nov. 6 reported an 87 percent increase in net provisions, to S$815 million, their highest level in 15 years, ""to remove uncertainty over residual weak oil and gas services exposures""."
Exxon,2017-11,"- At the end of September, DBS had S$3 billion of oil-and-gas support services non-performing assets, for which allowances of S$1.5 billion have been made."
Exxon,2017-11,"- The bank's net profit fell 23 percent to a five-year low of S$822 million, below the average estimate of S$1.13 billion from four analysts compiled by Thomson Reuters I/B/E/S."
Exxon,2017-11,Pakistan's Engro eyes 2019 start for new LNG terminal in Karachi - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-11,{{20171104T094037.102+0000}}Pakistan's Engro eyes 2019 start for new LNG terminal in KarachiBy Drazen Jorgic
Exxon,2017-11,"KARACHI, Nov 4 (Reuters) - Pakistani conglomerate Engro Corp expects to complete building its second liquefied natural gas (LNG) terminal in early 2019, a senior company official said, as Pakistan bets heavily on LNG imports to curb energy shortages."
Exxon,2017-11,"Engro built Pakistan's first LNG terminal in 2015 and is now finalising plans with Royal Dutch Shell , Fatima Group and trading house Gunvor for another terminal with capacity of 4.5 million tonnes per year."
Exxon,2017-11,"Pakistan has become a hot destination for global energy giants, with producers such as Exxon and traders like Vitol seeking partners to build terminals after Prime Minister Shahid Khaqan Abbasi re-oriented Pakistan's energy policy towards gas."
Exxon,2017-11,"A second terminal is due to come on line later this month, easing gas shortages that have hobbled Pakistan's manufacturing sector and wider economy for more than a decade. Private companies are racing to build several other terminals."
Exxon,2017-11,"Jahangir Piracha, chief executive of Engro's LNG unit, Elengy Terminal Pakistan, said his consortium expects to sign a final investment decision (FID) in the next few months and would then build the terminal in about a year."
Exxon,2017-11,"""The technical studies are all done. We are looking at early 2019 (to complete the project) if everything goes right,"" Piracha told Reuters in Karachi this week."
Exxon,2017-11,"A rival LNG terminal project by a six-member consortium that included ExxonMobil and Qatar Petroleum, appears to be in trouble after the American company pulled out, Pakistani officials said. ExxonMobil, however, remains very keen on Pakistan and is looking at other terminal projects. [nL8N1N546H]"
Exxon,2017-11,"Unlike Pakistan's first two terminals where the government guaranteed to buy all the gas due to be imported, the subsequent terminals are going to be entirely private ventures with no government off-take guarantees."
Exxon,2017-11,Engro's Piracha said the biggest challenge for the Engro consortium is to convince gas buyers such as power plants and factories to sign up before the project is on the ground.
Exxon,2017-11,"""Because there are so many people trying to develop a project, (local buyers) want to bet on the right horse. They don't want to sign up with you to find out that your project didn't come through,"" he said."
Exxon,2017-11,Piracha said this posed a problem for terminal developers who would prefer to have signed-up customers before making a final investment decision.
Exxon,2017-11,"""It's a bit of a chicken and egg story,"" Piracha said. ""My own feeling is that people want to see an investment and then they will sign up."""
Exxon,2017-11,"Piracha said other companies in the Engro group could sign up to be consumers from the terminal, which has the capacity for regasification of up to 600 million cubic feet per day, as could businesses from consortium partner Fatima, another major Pakistani conglomerate."
Exxon,2017-11,"{{20171104T094034.000+0000}}Pakistan's Engro eyes 2019 start for new LNG terminal in KarachiKARACHI, Nov 4 (Reuters)"

ExxonMobil, however, remains very keen on Pakistan and is looking at other terminal projects. [nL8N1N546H]"
Exxon,2017-11,"Unlike Pakistan's first two terminals where the government guaranteed to buy all the gas due to be imported, the subsequent terminals are going to be entirely private ventures with no government off-take guarantees."
Exxon,2017-11,Engro's Piracha said the biggest challenge for the Engro consortium is to convince gas buyers such as power plants and factories to sign up before the project is on the ground.
Exxon,2017-11,"""Because there are so many people trying to develop a project, (local buyers) want to bet on the right horse. They don't want to sign up with you to find out that your project didn't come through,"" he said."
Exxon,2017-11,Piracha said this posed a problem for terminal developers who would prefer to have signed-up customers before making a final investment decision.
Exxon,2017-11,"""It's a bit of a chicken and egg story,"" Piracha said. ""My own feeling is that people want to see an investment and then they will sign up."""
Exxon,2017-11,"Piracha said other companies in the Engro group could sign up to be consumers from the terminal, which has the capacity for regasification of up to 600 million cubic feet per day, as could businesses from consortium partner Fatima, another major Pakistani conglomerate."
