Exxon,2017-11,U.S. shale producers promise both higher output and returns - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-11,{{20171103T190227.262+0000}}U.S. shale producers promise both higher output and returnsBy Ernest Scheyder
Exxon,2017-11,"HOUSTON, Nov 3 (Reuters) - U.S. shale producers are telling investors impatient for better returns that they can keep boosting oil output aggressively and do so while still making money for shareholders."
Exxon,2017-11,"Investors have pushed top U.S. shale companies to focus on returns, rather than higher output, a move that threatened to slow the breakneck growth in supply sparked by the shale revolution in the world's top oil consumer."
Exxon,2017-11,"For the Organization of the Petroleum Exporting Countries, slower shale production gains would have been welcome. The cartel this year put caps on its members' production to end a supply glut and boost oil prices, only to find U.S. shale gains and record exports muting the impact of their curbs."
Exxon,2017-11,"But in comments during recent third-quarter earnings calls, shale executives signaled they expect to deliver both higher returns and output."
Exxon,2017-11,"At least seven of the largest U.S. shale companies, including Noble Energy Inc and Devon Energy Corp , forecast 10 percent or better production gains this quarter in the Permian Basin of West Texas and New Mexico, the largest U.S. oilfield."
Exxon,2017-11,"Underpinning the effort: Rising global oil demand and crude prices that are up about 30 percent since June lows. Shale producers are also proving they can drive output higher even after several last summer reported some Permian wells had begun delivering more natural gas, a sign of aging fields."
Exxon,2017-11,"""I'd like to think the industry is changing for the better,"" said Todd Heltman of wealth manager Neuberger Berman, which invests in shale producers. ""Investors are more focused on return metrics."""
Exxon,2017-11,Devon plans to boost oil production this quarter by 20 percent from the Permian and Oklahoma shale plays and spend less on each new well. [nL2N1N5147] [nL4N1N66JY]
Exxon,2017-11,"""We are taking the appropriate steps to become an industry leader with our disciplined approach to capital allocation,"" said Devon Chief Executive Dave Hager."
Exxon,2017-11,"U.S. shale output is expected to hit 6.1 million barrels of oil per day (bpd) this month, up 35 percent from a year earlier, according to the U.S. Energy Information Administration."
Exxon,2017-11,"The inventory of drilled-but-uncompleted wells, a backlog for future output, in September reached 7,120, up 42.6 percent from the year-ago period, and an all-time high. While the number of oil drilling rigs in the United States has slid in recent months, each rig's efficiency has jumped sharply in the past year."
Exxon,2017-11,"EOG Resources Inc boosted third-quarter production by 8 percent and swung to a $100 million profit, from a loss in the same period last year, helped in part by rising oil prices. CEO Bill Thomas said the company is aiming for 20 percent increase in U.S. crude output this year over last. Its stock is up nearly 17 percent since August.[nL2N1N821M]"
Exxon,2017-11,"Noble Energy forecast its fourth-quarter shale production will rise 15 percent to at least 102,000 bpd."
Exxon,2017-11,"""If you look at the growth from our Permian Basin drilling operations, you can see very substantial increases in oil production growth of about 15 percent,"" said Tim Dove, CEO of Pioneer Natural Resources Co ."
Exxon,2017-11,"Pioneer, one of the largest Permian oil producers, plans to boost its shale output by at least 16,000 bpd this quarter. The company's shares are up 15.4 percent since early August. [nL2N1N7253]"
Exxon,2017-11,"""We are excited about the trajectory of production growth in the upcoming quarters,"" said Vicki Hollub, CEO of Occidental Petroleum Corp , another top Permian producer. Oxy projects its Texas oil output will rise by more than 80,000 bpd by the end of 2018, to more than 200,000 bpd. [nL2N1N72CF]"
Exxon,2017-11,"Whiting Petroleum Corp , which operates in North Dakota's Bakken shale, plans a 10 percent jump in its fourth-quarter production.[nL2N1N02IO]"
Exxon,2017-11,"""We're confident about the areas in which we're drilling through to the end of the year and really, through the end of 2018,"" said Jim Volker, who retired as Whiting's CEO this week.[nL4N1MZ5UY]"
Exxon,2017-11,"Continental Resources Inc and Parsley Energy Inc , two other large U.S. shale producers, are due to report quarterly results next week."
Exxon,2017-11,"U.S. shale increases are keenly watched by OPEC, and likely will be in the spotlight when the group and other major producers meet on Nov. 30 in Vienna."
Exxon,2017-11,"Emmanuel Kachikwu, Nigeria's oil minister, warned at the last OPEC meeting in May that the group would ""sit down again and look at what process it is we need to do"" if U.S. shale output continues to weigh on global markets.[nL1N1IQ0AC]"
Exxon,2017-11,"Adding to the pressures, major oil companies that were late to recognize shale's potential have brought their own resources to bear. Chevron Corp and Exxon Mobil Corp are setting out aggressive plans for U.S. shale production, especially in the Permian.[nL2N1N20S2]"
Exxon,2017-11,"Exxon, which more than doubled its Permian holdings earlier this year, plans to boost the number of drilling rigs there by 50 percent, to 30, by the end of next year. By 2020, Exxon expects its Permian oil production to rise 45 percent.[nL2N1N20K7]"
Exxon,2017-11,"Chevron, which has operated in the Permian since the 1930s, recently added a 15th drilling rig in the Permian, with plans to add five more.[nL2N1N20NT]"
Exxon,2017-11,"""We'll be in a position to grow production for a period of years just from the shale,"" Chevron CEO John Watson said of the company's Permian operations."
Exxon,2017-11,BRIEF-Point Resources closes acquisition of ExxonMobil fields off Norway  - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-11,{{20171103T074546.997+0000}}BRIEF-Point Resources closes acquisition of ExxonMobil fields off Norway Nov 3 (Reuters) -
Exxon,2017-11,"* Point Resources as says has closed acquisition of the Exxonmobil-operated Balder, Ringhorne, Ringhorne east, Jotun and Forseti fields on the Norwegian continental shelf (NCS)"
Exxon,2017-11,"UPDATE 1-Threats to NAFTA cast doubt over Mexico's oil tenders, investment - Reuters News"
Exxon,2017-11,"{{20171103T005603.510+0000}}UPDATE 1-Threats to NAFTA cast doubt over Mexico's oil tenders, investment(Adds comment from oil regulator)"
Exxon,2017-11,"MEXICO CITY, Nov 2 (Reuters) - Uncertainty about the fate of the North American Free Trade Agreement (NAFTA) and investor protections it guarantees could crimp future investment in Mexico's oil industry, including a high-stakes January deepwater auction."
Exxon,2017-11,"Ahead of a fifth round of NAFTA talks in Mexico City in mid-November, Washington's tough demands that partners Canada and Mexico resist has clouded the future of the 23-year-old pact President Donald Trump has threatened to quit if he cannot get a better deal. [nL2N1MS0XB]"
Exxon,2017-11,"The January deepwater tender of 29 blocks holding some 4.2 billion barrels of prospective reserves, could suffer if concerns about NAFTA's future persuaded oil majors such as Chevron Corp and Exxon Mobil Corp to sit out the auction, oil executives and former government officials say."
Exxon,2017-11,"So far, 17 companies have begun the process of pre-qualifying for the auction."
Exxon,2017-11,"""Future investment without those investment protections of NAFTA will take into account the higher level of risk of any dispute not being settled in a more fair manner,"" Tim Callahan, Mexico country manager for Australia's BHP Billiton , told Reuters."
Exxon,2017-11,"Energy firms worry the end of NAFTA could eliminate the so-called Investor State Dispute Settlement, which allows such conflicts to be settled via international arbitrators, overriding contractual clauses that only reference local courts."
Exxon,2017-11,"Last December, BHP Billiton won a 60 percent stake in the $11 billion Trion field in the Gulf of Mexico, the flagship deepwater project of state-owned oil company Pemex."
Exxon,2017-11,"That same day, eight of 10 blocks were awarded in the deepwater auction, yielding investment commitments worth hundreds of millions of dollars in the first few years of the contracts alone by firms like U.S.-based Chevron and Murphy Oil."
Exxon,2017-11,"The auctions are part of a 2013 energy reform that ended Pemex's monopoly on oil and gas production. So far, the reform has secured investment pledges that will eventually be worth about $80 billion, the government says."
Exxon,2017-11,"Callahan, who heads the Mexican oil producer association's NAFTA committee, pointed to longstanding nationalist sentiment toward oil and a lack of legal precedents during the 75-year Pemex monopoly."
Exxon,2017-11,"""I don't think any of us want to be the first to test in the Mexican courts how they're going to rule on any disputes when it comes to oil,"" he said."
Exxon,2017-11,"Threats to NAFTA may force some U.S. oil firms to opt out of January's tenders, said former deputy energy minister Lourdes Melgar, an architect of the auctions. Some deem the investor dispute mechanism ""essential"" to protect investments, she added."
Exxon,2017-11,"Some of the biggest investments to date were made only after the government assured firms behind closed doors that any expropriation or administrative withdrawal of contracts could be appealed using the NAFTA resolution mechanism, said Carlos Pascual, a former U.S. ambassador to Mexico now at IHS Markit."
Exxon,2017-11,"The assurances were made before Trump's surprise election win and company concerns over investor protections lasted ""up until the last minute"" before bids were submitted, Pascual said."
Exxon,2017-11,"Without NAFTA, investment disputes could fall to Mexican courts, which unsettles some firms concerned that local judges are often susceptible to bribes or intimidation, oil company executives and former officials say."
Exxon,2017-11,"""It's a fight for the oil and gas dollar now, and if the companies aren't treated fairly, then there's lots of other places to go,"" said Craig Steinke, head of Canada-based Renaissance Oil Corp , a company that has won five onshore contracts in Mexico."
Exxon,2017-11,"Even under the oil contracts' administrative withdrawal clause, companies are entitled to an audience to present their case, the participation of an independent expert and there are no one-person decisions, said Juan Carlos Zepeda, head of oil regulator CNH, which is in charge of supervising the contracts."
Exxon,2017-11,"Energy Minister Pedro Joaquin Coldwell told Reuters that even without NAFTA protections, respect for due process was embedded in Mexico's legal system. He added that Mexico has more than a dozen other bilateral investment treaties with similar protections as NAFTA, a point that several oil executives who have spoken to Reuters in private also make."
Exxon,2017-11,"However, leftist presidential hopeful Andres Manuel Lopez Obrador, who has led early polls for next July's election, has a different message."
Exxon,2017-11,Lopez Obrador promises to review signed oil contracts and his top energy advisor Rocio Nahle said foreign companies should not bank on bypassing local courts.
Exxon,2017-11,"""They need to be careful ... and respect Mexico's laws because this is Mexican territory,"" said Nahle, who also leads Lopez Obrador's party in the lower house of Congress."
Exxon,2017-11,"CORRECTED-Threats to NAFTA cast doubt over Mexico's oil tenders, investment - Reuters News"
Exxon,2017-11,"{{20171103T003320.879+0000}}CORRECTED-Threats to NAFTA cast doubt over Mexico's oil tenders, investment(Corrects Carlos Pascual's employer to IHS Markit, from IHS Global Energy)"

Exxon,2017-11,"HOUSTON, Nov 2 (Reuters) - A 78,000 barrel-per-day (bpd) reformer was heavily damaged in a fire at ExxonMobil Corp's 502,500 bpd Baton Rouge, Louisiana, refinery, sources familiar with plant operations said on Thursday. A leak was being repaired on the unit when the fire broke out early on Wednesday, the sources said."
Exxon,2017-11,"There is no timeline for repairing the reformer, which is called the Powerformer."
Exxon,2017-11,An Exxon spokeswoman did not reply to a request for comment.
Exxon,2017-11,"Early on Wednesday morning, the reformer, which converts refining by-products into octane-boosting components of gasoline, was roped off due to the leak when the fire broke out, the sources said."
Exxon,2017-11,"The refinery's 210,000 bpd crude distillation unit (CDU), the largest of four doing the primary refining of crude oil and providing feedstocks for all other units, was taken out of production to stop the flow of feed to the reformer shortly after the fire erupted."

Exxon,2017-11,UPDATE 2-Valero a gasoline buyer on U.S. East Coast after Pembroke outage -sources - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-11,{{20171102T194643.598+0000}}UPDATE 2-Valero a gasoline buyer on U.S. East Coast after Pembroke outage -sources(Adds Exxon purchases)
Exxon,2017-11,"NEW YORK, Nov 2 (Reuters) - Valero Energy was buying gasoline cargoes for spot delivery in the U.S. East Coast after an outage at its 270,000 barrels per day (bpd) Pembroke refinery in Wales earlier this week, two trade sources said on Thursday."
Exxon,2017-11,"Valero, the largest U.S. independent refiner, typically sells gasoline barrels from their Pembroke refinery into the New York Harbor market, traders said."
Exxon,2017-11,"Exxon Mobil was also buying prompt gasoline barrels in the New York harbor on Thursday, traders said."
Exxon,2017-11,"The purchases come as supplies in the U.S. East Coast have been squeezed amid lower transatlantic imports and fewer barrels being sent via pipeline from the Gulf Coast refining hub. U.S. Midwest prices have also soared, pulling barrels away from the New York harbor. [nL4N1N16XB]"
Exxon,2017-11,Gasoline prices in the New York Harbor have surged and traded about 6 cents a gallon above benchmark futures for delivery in December on the New York Mercantile Exchange on Thursday.
Exxon,2017-11,"The U.S. gasoline crack spread - a key metric in refining margins - continues to surge above five-year highs seasonally. It rose as much as 7.7 percent to $20.27 a barrel on Thursday, after ending the session at around $19.79."
Exxon,2017-11,"The 90,000 bpd fluid catalytic converter (FCC) at Pembroke was shut unexpectedly earlier this week, three trade sources said. It was not immediately clear what caused the shutdown or when the unit would be restarted."
Exxon,2017-11,"Traders said Valero was also looking to sell vacuum gasoil, the feedstock used to feed the FCC."
Exxon,2017-11,A spokeswoman for the refinery declined to comment on the plant's day to day operations.
Exxon,2017-11,"Valero purchased the prompt barrels at 6 cents per gallon above benchmark futures, one East Coast trader said. Exxon, meanwhile, did not ship barrels over from Europe, prompting the company to buy barrels in the Philadelphia region and move it west since its Joliet plant was down."
Exxon,2017-11,"Exxon said last week planned maintenance is continuing on several units at the 238,600 bpd Joliet, Illinois refinery. [nFWN1N01DR]"
Exxon,2017-11,Gasoline refining margins in northwest Europe extended their gains on Thursday on the back of the outage. [nL8N1N8844]

Exxon,2017-11,Quarter of oil refineries risk closure under climate goals -report - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-11,"{{20171102T000101.058+0000}}Quarter of oil refineries risk closure under climate goals -report* Refining profits to shrivel as demand drops, report says"
Exxon,2017-11,"LONDON, Nov 2 (Reuters) - A quarter of the world's oil refineries risk closure by 2035 if governments meet targets to limit fossil fuel burning in the fight against global warming, a report released on Thursday said."
Exxon,2017-11,"A surge in electric vehicle sales and higher efficiency in internal combustion and jet engines are expected to slow demand growth for fuels such as gasoline, diesel and aviation fuel in the coming decades, potentially putting pressure on refining profits."
Exxon,2017-11,"At the same time, governments around the world are set to introduce legislation in the coming years to limit emissions of heat-capturing carbon dioxide into the atmosphere in order to meet targets set at a U.N-backed Paris conference in 2015."
Exxon,2017-11,"As a result, companies such as Chevron , Royal Dutch Shell , France' Total and China's largest refiner Sinopec could see profits from refining drop by 70 percent or more over the period, according to the report co-authored by environment thinktank Carbon Tracker, Swedish investment fund AP7 and Danish pension fund PKA."
Exxon,2017-11,The study is based on the International Energy Agency's 450 Scenario to limit global warming to 2 degrees Celsius under which oil demand declines by 23 percent between 2020 and 2035.
Exxon,2017-11,"Under this scenario, despite new refinery additions in Asia and the Middle East, only 62 percent of global capacity will be required to meet demand compared with around 80 percent today. Profits from converting crude oil into refined products will also shrink."
Exxon,2017-11,"That in turn means that approximately one quarter of the 2016 refining capacity, the equivalent of some 24.7 million barrels per day of oil demand, will need to be closed, the report said."
Exxon,2017-11,"The closures would likely be more pronounced in developed economies where oil demand is expected to peak earlier than in developing economies. Also, modern, complex refineries that can produce more high quality and cleaner fuels are likely to fare better than older plants."
Exxon,2017-11,"""The consequences of achieving a 2 degree Celsius world are far more detrimental to the refining sector than the upstream sector, as it results in structural over-capacity and associated poor refining margin environment, which can only be addressed by sustained capacity rationalisation,"" said Alan Gelder, vice president for research at Edinburgh-based consultancy Wood Mackenzie which took part in the report."
Exxon,2017-11,Meeting the emission reduction targets however seems distant today. A report published on Tuesday said global emissions are set to be 30 percent higher than the target needed by 2030.[nL8N1N640X]
Exxon,2017-11,"While oil companies including Shell have acknowledged that demand for some fuels such as gasoline could peak by the end of the 2020s, they expect demand for oil to remain strong for decades from heavy transport, aviation and chemical production."
Exxon,2017-11,"The authors of the report estimate that overall earnings before interest, taxes, depreciation and amortization (EBITDA) for refiners could fall by over 50 percent by 2035 from around $147 billion in 2015."
Exxon,2017-11,"""We consider that prospective investors should be wary of all new refinery investments,"" the report said."
Exxon,2017-11,"""When demand growth stalls and turns negative, new investments will carry the risk of failing to earn an adequate return."""
Exxon,2017-11,Carbon Tracker and a group of investors warned in a report earlier this year that oil giants risk spending trillions by 2025 on oil and gas projects that won't be feasible under the international climate targets. [nL8N1JI1P9]
Exxon,2017-11,"{{20171101T183511.425+0000}}UPDATE 1-Exxon Baton Rouge refinery reformer shut after fire -sources(Adds company statement, details about unit, background on refinery)"
Exxon,2017-11,"HOUSTON, Nov 1 (Reuters) - A 78,000 barrel-per-day (bpd) reformer was shut on Wednesday by an early-morning fire at ExxonMobil Corp's 502,500 bpd Baton Rouge, Louisiana, refinery, said sources familiar with plant operations."
Exxon,2017-11,"The fire broke out on the unit, called the Powerformer, at about 2:30 a.m. CDT (0730 GMT) on Wednesday, the sources said."
Exxon,2017-11,"""On-site responders contained the fire to the area where it occurred and there were no injuries,"" said Exxon spokeswoman Lana Venable. ""There was no community impact."""
Exxon,2017-11,Venable did not identify the unit where the fire broke out.
Exxon,2017-11,"Energy industry intelligence service Genscape said the refinery's 210,000 bpd crude distillation unit (CDU), the largest of four at the plant, was shut following the fire, though the blaze was not near the CDU."
Exxon,2017-11,"The reformer, which has two 39,000 bpd production trains, converts refining by-products into octane-boosting components blended into gasoline."
Exxon,2017-11,This is the second fire on a unit involved in gasoline production in the past year at the refinery.
Exxon,2017-11,"On Nov. 22, 2016, a fire broke out in the alkylation unit when workers disassembled a valve. Four workers were critically injured in the blaze. In May, the U.S. Occupational Safety and Health Administration fined Exxon $165,000 for safety violations."
Exxon,2017-11,CDUs do the primary refining of crude oil in a refinery and provide feedstock to all other units.
Exxon,2017-11,"Alkylation units, through a different process, also convert refining by-products into octane boosting components of gasoline."
Exxon,2017-11,"{{20171101T151834.074+0000}}Exxon Baton Rouge refinery reformer shut after fire -sourcesHOUSTON, Nov 1 (Reuters) - A 78,000 barrel-per-day (bpd) reformer was shut on Wednesday by an early-morning fire at ExxonMobil Corp's 502,500 bpd Baton Rouge, Louisiana, refinery, said sources familiar with plant operations."
Exxon,2017-11,"The fire broke out on the unit, called the Powerformer, at about 2:30 a.m. CDT (0730 GMT) on Wednesday, the sources said. No injuries were reported from the blaze."
Exxon,2017-11,"{{20171101T121107.770+0000}}UPDATE 2-Exxon says fire contained at Baton Rouge, La. refinery(Adds details from Genscape, Exxon no comment)"
Exxon,2017-11,"Nov 1 (Reuters) - ExxonMobil Corp said on Wednesday that a fire that occurred at its 502,500 barrel-per-day (bpd) Baton Rouge, Louisiana refinery on Wednesday morning was contained to the area."
Exxon,2017-11,"There were no injuries and no impact to community, a company spokeswoman said."
Exxon,2017-11,"The 210,000-bpd crude section of the refinery, Pipestill 10, was shut down following the incident, although the fire occurred in a different part of the plant, energy industry intelligence service Genscape said. [nIGB3E99A5]"
Exxon,2017-11,"Asked to comment about which unit was involved, Exxon said it is the company's policy not to comment on specific unit operations."

Exxon,2017-11,UPDATE 2-Australia's Oil Search buys into promising Alaska oil find - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-11,{{20171101T064826.194+0000}}UPDATE 2-Australia's Oil Search buys into promising Alaska oil find* Spain's Repsol sees field holding 1.2 bln barrels of oil
Exxon,2017-11,"MELBOURNE, Nov 1 (Reuters) - Australia's Oil Search Ltd has agreed to buy stakes in a huge oil find in Alaska for $400 million, in a surprise push to diversify from its sweet spot of gas in Papua New Guinea."
Exxon,2017-11,"Oil Search will pick up stakes in three oil blocks from privately owned U.S. firms Armstrong Energy and GMT Exploration giving it a roughly 26 percent holding in the Nanushuk play, co-owned by Spain's Repsol SA ."
Exxon,2017-11,"The play includes the Horseshoe block, which hit oil in March in what Repsol called the biggest U.S. onshore find in 30 years. It estimated the field could hold 1.2 billion barrels. [nFWN1GM0QP]"
Exxon,2017-11,"Oil Search bought in assuming the field holds 500 million barrels, expecting production to begin in 2023, with output to plateau at 80,000 to 120,000 barrels per day."
Exxon,2017-11,"""With the quality of the assets, the fact that they're tier 1, and the fact that we've gone in very conservatively against what Repsol are saying, I think we can demonstrate to the market that this will be a super deal for Oil Search in the medium term,"" Oil Search Chief Executive Peter Botten told Reuters."
Exxon,2017-11,"Investors were nervous about the $8 billion company's move into a region where it has no experience and which is dominated by giants like BP and ExxonMobil Corp , sending its shares down 3 percent, especially after it gave up on a push into Kurdistan."
Exxon,2017-11,Other Australian oil and gas producers rose more than 1 percent on Wednesday.
Exxon,2017-11,"""Questions will inevitably be asked about Oil Search's competitive advantage to play in Alaska until it proves its operational capability there,"" said Saul Kavonic, an analyst with energy consultants Wood Mackenzie."
Exxon,2017-11,"RBC analyst Ben Wilson said the move was well-timed near the bottom of the oil price cycle and with some of the appraisal work on the field already done. He said it had ""good prospects"" as the oil was high-grade."
Exxon,2017-11,"Botten began working on the deal eight months ago when oil prices were about 20 percent lower than now and said Oil Search managed to get the asset despite higher-priced interest from others in nearby fields, whom he declined to name."
Exxon,2017-11,"The owners of the neighbouring fields are ConocoPhillips , ExxonMobil and Italy's ENI ."
Exxon,2017-11,Oil Search has the option of doubling its stake in the Alaskan assets for a further $450 million. It plans to fund the deal from its cash reserves.
Exxon,2017-11,Oil Search will work with oilfield services giant Halliburton Co and Armstrong before taking over as operator of the assets in June 2018.

Exxon,2017-11,"UPDATE 2-Exxon Mobil, PDC Energy settle with U.S., states over air pollution claims - Reuters News"
Exxon,2017-11,"{{20171031T202148.172+0000}}UPDATE 2-Exxon Mobil, PDC Energy settle with U.S., states over air pollution claims(Adds PDC comment in paragraph 6)"
Exxon,2017-11,"WASHINGTON, Oct 31 (Reuters) - Exxon Mobil Corp and PDC Energy Inc will each pay a $2.5 million civil penalty to settle charges by the federal government and several states alleging the companies violated laws aimed at reducing air pollution, the U.S. Justice Department said on Tuesday."
Exxon,2017-11,"The settlement between Exxon and the department, the Environmental Protection Agency and the state of Louisiana alleges the company violated the Clean Air Act when it failed to properly operate and monitor industrial flares at eight of its petrochemical facilities in Texas and Louisiana."
Exxon,2017-11,"In addition to the penalty, it agreed to invest nearly $300 million to install new air pollution monitoring technology."
Exxon,2017-11,The PDC settlement with the federal government and the state of Colorado also relates to Clean Air Act violations stemming from emissions of volatile organic compounds from its oil and gas exploration and production businesses.
Exxon,2017-11,"Exxon denied any wrongdoing in the settlement, and its spokesman Aaron Stryk said the company worked closely with the government to resolve the matter."
Exxon,2017-11,"PDC President and Chief Executive Bart Brookman said the agreement resulted from months of conversations with state and EPA regulators. In its settlement, PDC denied any liability."
Exxon,2017-11,The company also agreed to spend about $18 million on systems upgrades and another $1.7 million to mitigate the problems.
Exxon,2017-11,"Exxon Mobil, PDC Energy settle with U.S., states over air pollution claims - Reuters News"
Exxon,2017-11,"{{20171031T173832.859+0000}}Exxon Mobil, PDC Energy settle with U.S., states over air pollution claimsWASHINGTON, Oct 31 (Reuters) - Exxon Mobil Corp and PDC Energy Inc will each pay a $2.5 million civil penalty to settle charges by the federal government and several states alleging the companies violated laws that aim to reduce air pollution, the U.S. Justice Department said Tuesday."
Exxon,2017-11,"The settlement between Exxon and the department, the Environmental Protection Agency and the state of Louisiana alleges the company violated the Clean Air Act when it failed to properly operate and monitor industrial flares at some of its petrochemical facilities."
Exxon,2017-11,The PDC settlement with the federal government and the state of Colorado also relates to Clean Air Act violations stemming from emissions of volatile organic compounds from its oil and gas exploration and production businesses.
Exxon,2017-11,"Total, Edison sign lease for oil and gas exploration off Greece - Reuters News"
Exxon,2017-11,"{{20171031T153933.144+0000}}Total, Edison sign lease for oil and gas exploration off GreeceBy Karolina Tagaris"
Exxon,2017-11,"ATHENS, Oct 31 (Reuters) - A consortium led by France's Total moved a step closer to exploring for oil and gas off Greece after signing a lease on Tuesday with the government for a block in the Ionian Sea."
Exxon,2017-11,Greece wants to tap into its limited oil reserves to reduce dependence on oil imports and boost public finances.
Exxon,2017-11,"It awarded the contract to the Total consortium, which also includes Greece's biggest oil refiner Hellenic Petroleum and Italy's Edison , in October 2016."
Exxon,2017-11,"""Undoubtedly it is a vote of confidence in the Greek economy,"" Energy Minister George Stathakis said of the agreement on Tuesday."
Exxon,2017-11,"Total will operate the block with a 50 percent stake, while Edison and Hellenic Petroleum will each hold 25 percent. The agreement must be ratified by Greece's parliament before exploration work can begin."
Exxon,2017-11,"Western Greece is a frontier, underexplored area and very little data exists on its hydrocarbon potential."
Exxon,2017-11,"Bernard Clement, a senior Total executive for the Caspian and Southern Europe, said it would maintain ""realistic expectations"" before obtaining data."
Exxon,2017-11,Total has shown interest in the eastern Mediterranean following major gas discoveries off Israel and Egypt. It is currently drilling for oil off Cyprus.
Exxon,2017-11,"Together with Hellenic Petroleum in a consortium led by U.S. oil major Exxon Mobil , Total has also expressed interest in exploration at two sites off Crete, prompting Greece to launch a tender."
Exxon,2017-11,"Greece, like other European countries, relies on Russian gas imports which account for over 60 percent of supplies. Russia covers about a third of Greece's oil needs."
Exxon,2017-11,Athens also wants to attract investment into the oil industry as it tries to emerge from years of economic crisis.
Exxon,2017-11,"During a meeting with U.S. President Donald Trump this month, Greek Prime Minister Alexis Tsipras said Athens wanted U.S. investment in energy too, and it planned to set up a taskforce to overcome red tape."
Exxon,2017-11,"""It helps a lot to keep the bureaucracy moving if you have a clear message from the top that the answer to investors should be 'Yes',"" U.S. ambassador to Greece, Geoffrey Pyatt, told Reuters."
Exxon,2017-11,"Greece has one LNG terminal off Athens, where it imports Algerian gas, but an official at state-run gas firm DEPA said it plans to invite U.S. companies to ship LNG there for the first time."
Exxon,2017-11,"It is also developing a floating storage and regasification unit (FSRU) off Alexandroupolis, a city close to the Turkish and Bulgarian borders near where EU-backed pipelines are being built to cut reliance on Russian gas."
Exxon,2017-11,"""Our vision for Greece (is) as a European energy hub,"" said Pyatt, a former U.S. ambassador to Ukraine."
Exxon,2017-11,"The FSRU, with an estimated annual capacity of 6.1 billion cubic metres, will seek to supply gas to southeastern Europe via the Interconnector Greece-Bulgaria (IGB) pipeline, which is due to begin construction next year."
Exxon,2017-11,"The IGB and the FSRU could be connected to the Trans-Adriatic Pipeline which is being built to carry Caspian gas to European markets, which currently depends on Russian oil giant Gazprom for a third of its supply."
Exxon,2017-11,"""You have several American companies that are looking at the FSRU,"" Pyatt said. ""We very much hope to see an American company also become involved."""
